---
title: String | Healthie API Docs
source_url:
  html: https://docs.gethealthie.com/reference/2026-01-01/scalars/string/index
  md: https://docs.gethealthie.com/reference/2026-01-01/scalars/string/index.md
---

The \`String\` scalar type represents textual data, represented as UTF-8 character sequences. The String type is most often used by GraphQL to represent free-form human-readable text.

## Definition

```
"""
The `String` scalar type represents textual data, represented as UTF-8 character sequences. The String type is most often used by GraphQL to represent free-form human-readable text.
"""
scalar String
```
